Grammar:
 equality_expr -> <34> relational_expr(exp)    { v = exp; }
                | <35> equality_expr EQ relational_expr
                | <36> equality_expr NE relational_expr;
 stmt_list -> <4> statement
            | <5> stmt_list statement;
 relational_expr -> <37> add_expr(exp)    { v = exp; }
                  | <38> relational_expr LT add_expr
                  | <39> relational_expr GT add_expr
                  | <40> relational_expr GE add_expr
                  | <41> relational_expr LE add_expr;
 statement -> <6> expr_stmt
            | <7> select_stmt
            | <8> loop_stmt
            | <9> decl
            | <10> per_def_func;
 prime_expr -> <57> ID(id)    { v = id; }
             | <58> NUM_CONST(number)    { v = number; }
             | <59> STR_CONST(string)    { v = string; }
             | <60> CHAR_CONST(charType)    { v = charType; }
             | <61> BOOL_CONST(bool)    { v = bool; }
             | <62> OPENPA expr(exp) CLOSEPA    { v = exp; };
 assign_op -> <51> ASSIGN(assign)    { v = assign; };
 logical_and_expr -> <32> equality_expr(exp)    { v = exp; }
                   | <33> logical_and_expr(andExp) AND equality_expr(eqExp)    { v = null; };
 loop_stmt -> <16> WHILE OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDWHILE
            | <17> DO COLON compound_stmt ENDDO OPENPA expr CLOSEPA
            | <18> FOR OPENPA opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDFOR;
 conditional_expr -> <29> logical_or_expr(exp)    { v = exp; };
 compound_stmt -> <1> stmt_list
                | <2> ;
 cast_expr -> <49> unary_expr(exp)    { v = exp; }
            | <50> OPENPA type CLOSEPA cast_expr;
 unary_op -> <52> NOT(not)    { v = not; }
           | <53> UNARY_INCREMENT(increment)    { v = increment; }
           | <54> UNARY_DECREMENT(decrement)    { v = decrement; };
 decl -> <3> ID(id) COLON type(type) ASSIGN conditional_expr(value) SEMICOL    { v = SymbolTable.setAttributes(id, type, value); };
 opt_expr -> <19> expr
           | <20> ;
Sprogram' -> <63> program;
 per_def_func -> <11> OUT OPENPA expr CLOSEPA SEMICOL;
 add_expr -> <42> mult_expr(exp)    { v = exp; }
           | <43> add_expr PLUS mult_expr
           | <44> add_expr SUB mult_expr;
 expr_stmt -> <12> expr SEMICOL
            | <13> SEMICOL;
 expr -> <21> assign_expr(exp)    { v = exp; };
 program -> <0> STARTINPUT COLON compound_stmt ENDINPUT;
 logical_or_expr -> <30> logical_and_expr(exp)    { v = exp; }
                  | <31> logical_or_expr(orExp) OR logical_and_expr(andExp)    { v = null; };
 select_stmt -> <14> IF OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENIF    { v = null; symbolTable.exitCurrentScope(); }
              | <15> IF OPENPA expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ELSE COLON compound_stmt ENIF    { v = null; symbolTable.exitCurrentScope(); };
 unary_expr -> <55> prime_expr(exp)    { v = exp; }
             | <56> unary_op cast_expr;
 mult_expr -> <45> cast_expr(exp)    { v = exp; }
            | <46> mult_expr MUL cast_expr
            | <47> mult_expr DIV cast_expr
            | <48> mult_expr MOD cast_expr;
 assign_expr -> <27> conditional_expr(exp)    { v = exp; }
              | <28> unary_expr(unaryExp) assign_op(assignOP) assign_expr(assignExp)    { v = SymbolTable.updateAttributes(unaryExp, assignOP, assignExp); };
 type -> <22> INT(type)    { v = type; }
       | <23> STR(type)    { v = type; }
       | <24> FLOAT(type)    { v = type; }
       | <25> BOOL(type)    { v = type; }
       | <26> CHAR(type)    { v = type; };

State 0:
    program' -> * program, {EOF}

State 1:
    program -> STARTINPUT * COLON compound_stmt ENDINPUT, {EOF}

State 2:
    program' -> program *, {EOF}

State 3:
    program -> STARTINPUT COLON * compound_stmt ENDINPUT, {EOF}

State 4:
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {EQ}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {NE}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {NE}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {EQ}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {SEMICOL}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {SEMICOL}
    logical_and_expr -> equality_expr *, {OR}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {AND}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {AND}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * NE relational_expr, {OR}
    logical_and_expr -> equality_expr *, {AND}
    equality_expr -> equality_expr * EQ relational_expr, {OR}
    logical_and_expr -> equality_expr *, {SEMICOL}

State 5:
    stmt_list -> stmt_list * statement, {STR_CONST, UNARY_INCREMENT, DO, NOT, FOR, ID, OPENPA, OUT, BOOL_CONST, IF, SEMICOL, CHAR_CONST, UNARY_DECREMENT, NUM_CONST, WHILE}
    stmt_list -> stmt_list * statement, {ENDINPUT}
    compound_stmt -> stmt_list *, {ENDINPUT}

State 6:
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {DIV}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {LT}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {GE}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {OR}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {GT}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {LE}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {AND}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {MUL}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {PLUS}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {SEMICOL}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {ASSIGN}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {MOD}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {SUB}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {NE}
    prime_expr -> STR_CONST *, {EQ}

State 7:
    unary_op -> UNARY_INCREMENT *, {STR_CONST, BOOL_CONST, UNARY_INCREMENT, NOT, CHAR_CONST, UNARY_DECREMENT, ID, NUM_CONST, OPENPA}

State 8:
    equality_expr -> relational_expr *, {OR}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LT add_expr, {OR}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GE add_expr, {OR}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GT add_expr, {OR}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LT add_expr, {GT}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GT add_expr, {GT}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LE add_expr, {OR}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LE add_expr, {AND}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LE add_expr, {GE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GE add_expr, {GT}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GE add_expr, {AND}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LE add_expr, {GT}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LE add_expr, {SEMICOL}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GE add_expr, {SEMICOL}
    equality_expr -> relational_expr *, {EQ}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GT add_expr, {SEMICOL}
    equality_expr -> relational_expr *, {NE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LT add_expr, {SEMICOL}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LE add_expr, {EQ}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GE add_expr, {EQ}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GT add_expr, {EQ}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LT add_expr, {EQ}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GT add_expr, {GE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GT add_expr, {AND}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LT add_expr, {AND}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GE add_expr, {GE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LE add_expr, {NE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LT add_expr, {GE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GT add_expr, {NE}
    equality_expr -> relational_expr *, {AND}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GE add_expr, {NE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LT add_expr, {NE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GE add_expr, {LT}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LE add_expr, {LT}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LT add_expr, {LE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GT add_expr, {LE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LT add_expr, {LT}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GT add_expr, {LT}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * GE add_expr, {LE}
    relational_expr -> relational_expr * LE add_expr, {LE}
    equality_expr -> relational_expr *, {SEMICOL}

State 9:
    loop_stmt -> DO * COLON compound_stmt ENDDO OPENPA expr CLOSEPA, {ENDINPUT}
    loop_stmt -> DO * COLON compound_stmt ENDDO OPENPA expr CLOSEPA, {STR_CONST, UNARY_INCREMENT, DO, NOT, FOR, ID, OPENPA, OUT, BOOL_CONST, IF, SEMICOL, CHAR_CONST, UNARY_DECREMENT, NUM_CONST, WHILE}

State 10:
    unary_op -> NOT *, {STR_CONST, BOOL_CONST, UNARY_INCREMENT, NOT, CHAR_CONST, UNARY_DECREMENT, ID, NUM_CONST, OPENPA}

State 11:
    stmt_list -> statement *, {ENDINPUT}
    stmt_list -> statement *, {STR_CONST, UNARY_INCREMENT, DO, NOT, FOR, ID, OPENPA, OUT, BOOL_CONST, IF, SEMICOL, CHAR_CONST, UNARY_DECREMENT, NUM_CONST, WHILE}

State 12:
    unary_expr -> prime_expr *, {OR}
    unary_expr -> prime_expr *, {GT}
    unary_expr -> prime_expr *, {LE}
    unary_expr -> prime_expr *, {LT}

    unary_expr -> prime_expr *, {NE}

    unary_expr -> prime_expr *, {ASSIGN}

State 13:
    loop_stmt -> FOR * OPENPA opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDFOR, {ENDINPUT}
    loop_stmt -> FOR * OPENPA opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr SEMICOL opt_expr CLOSEPA COLON compound_stmt ENDFOR, {STR_CONST, UNARY_INCREMENT, DO, NOT, FOR, ID, OPENPA, OUT, BOOL_CONST, IF, SEMICOL, CHAR_CONST, UNARY_DECREMENT, NUM_CONST, WHILE}

State 14:

State 15:
    per_def_func -> OUT * OPENPA expr CLOSEPA SEMICOL, {ENDINPUT}

State 16:
    logical_or_expr -> logical_and_expr *, {OR}
    logical_and_expr -> logical_and_expr * AND equality_expr, {SEMICOL}

    logical_and_expr -> logical_and_expr * AND equality_expr, {OR}
    logical_and_expr -> logical_and_expr * AND equality_expr, {AND}

State 17:
    statement -> loop_stmt *, {ENDINPUT}
    statement -> loop_stmt *, {STR_CONST, UNARY_INCREMENT, DO, NOT, FOR, ID, OPENPA, OUT, BOOL_CONST, IF, SEMICOL, CHAR_CONST, UNARY_DECREMENT, NUM_CONST, WHILE}

State 18:
    assign_expr -> conditional_expr *, {SEMICOL}

State 19:
    program -> STARTINPUT COLON compound_stmt * ENDINPUT, {EOF}
